‚Źļ¬†User answered Claude's questions:
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ There's no Azure region list in the code today, and pricing.json holds 
     rates for one region only (West Europe, EUR). The region dropdown will be a
     curated list of Azure regions (+ an 'Unknown / Not in list' option). How 
     should the per-tier COST RATES vary by the account's selected region? ‚Üí 
     Only regions in the json
     ¬∑ The Arius.Api backend runs in Docker and can only see paths mounted into 
     the container ‚ÄĒ it cannot browse your host filesystem. The local path 
     stored is the path AS THE API SEES IT. How should the local-path '[...]' 
     picker work? ‚Üí Server-side browser

‚Źļ Both decisions are clear:
  - Region pricing ‚Üí "Only regions in the json": restructure pricing.json to be
  region-keyed; the dropdown is derived from its region keys + "Unknown". This
  makes pricing.json the single source of truth ("owns the pricing json").
  - Folder picker ‚Üí "Server-side browser": new backend directory-listing
  endpoint + an Angular folder picker over paths the API can see.

  Let me verify how the Mediator is wired at the app level vs per-repo (this
  determines how the CostQuery and regions endpoints dispatch without needlessly
  authenticating to blob storage).

  Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

‚Źļ I now have full ground-truth on every relevant file and both design decisions.
  One decisive architectural finding: IMediator exists only inside 
  per-repository providers (AddMediator() runs per-repo in
  RepositoryProviderRegistry.BuildAsync, line 135) ‚ÄĒ there is no app-level
  mediator. So the region list (needed before any repo exists, during account
  creation) must come from a plain app-level endpoint reading the embedded
  pricing.json, while the per-repo CostQuery dispatches through the repo
  provider like StatisticsQuery does.

  Let me write the plan.

  library exposes IQuery/IQueryHandler (the codebase currently only uses

‚Źļ Confirmed: Mediator 3.0.2 (martinothamar) ‚ÄĒ it exposes
  IQuery<T>/IQueryHandler<,> (the codebase just hasn't used them yet; it uses
  ICommand + IStreamQuery). mediator.Send(IQuery<T>) works the same way. So
  IQuery is the right, read-correct choice. And I fully agree the math belongs
  in Core. Let me answer your questions and rework the plan.

  Who owns what:
  - Rates ‚Üí Core's new Shared/Pricing/PricingCatalog (region-keyed pricing.json,
  single source of truth).
  - Per-tier stored sizes ‚Üí the existing StatisticsQuery (chunk index).
  - The cost math ‚Üí the new CostQuery handler in Core: it dispatches
  StatisticsQuery, multiplies each tier's stored size by that region's
  storagePerGBPerMonth (using the same 1024¬≥ GiB convention as
  RestoreCostCalculator), and returns finished per-tier costs + grand total +
  currency. The frontend does zero arithmetic ‚ÄĒ it just renders.

  Let me update the plan accordingly.

     ‚Ēā Plan: Storage Accounts management + region-aware Cost Calculator        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Context                                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Two related changes to the Arius.Web Angular SPA and its Arius.Api /    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Arius.Core .NET backend (Mediator/CQRS, SQLite app DB):                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Group 1 ‚ÄĒ Storage accounts & repos: Today storage accounts are        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā second-class ‚ÄĒ they're only created inline in the New/Add-repo wizards, ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā can never be edited, and carry no Azure region. The Overview has no     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā place to see or manage them. Meanwhile the repo Properties page shows   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā an "Account key" field that doesn't even belong to a repo (and isn't    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā persisted). We surface accounts on the Overview, add a region to each   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā account, make accounts editable via a flyout, and clean up the          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Properties page.                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Group 2 ‚ÄĒ Cost calculator: The Statistics tab's "Stored size by tier" ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā section shows size but no cost. We add a region-aware storage-cost      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā calculator in Core (exposed via a Mediator CostQuery, alongside ‚ÄĒ not   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā replacing ‚ÄĒ the existing RestoreCostCalculator), and a shared Angular   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā CostCalculator component that renders the redesigned cost-aware tier    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā breakdown (per the design handoff in                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā scratchpad/design_handoff/.../Statistics Tab v2.dc.html).               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Decisions confirmed with the user                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 1. Region pricing = "only regions in the json." pricing.json becomes    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā region-keyed and is the single source of truth. The region dropdown     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā lists exactly the regions present in the json + an "Unknown / Not in    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā list" option. Today that means [westeurope, Unknown]; the list grows as ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā regions are added to the json. Rates select by the account's region;    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Unknown/missing ‚Üí fall back to the default region.                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 2. Local-path picker = server-side browser. A new backend endpoint      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā lists directories as the Arius.Api host/container sees them (mounted    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā volumes under Docker; real folders when run locally). A [...] button    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā opens a small folder picker over that.                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Key facts that shape the plan (verified)                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Account key is already account-scoped in the DB                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (storage_accounts.account_key) and the API DTOs. The repo Properties    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā "Account key" field is vestigial ‚ÄĒ save() never sends it. So Group 1    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā #2's "reflect in the DB" needs no DB change; it's a frontend removal.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - No UpdateAccount exists (DB method, endpoint, or DTO) and no location ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā column ‚ÄĒ both are net-new for the edit-account flyout + region.         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Mediator lives only per-repo (AddMediator() in                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā RepositoryProviderRegistry.BuildAsync). The regions list (used during   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā account creation, before any repo) must be a plain app-level endpoint.  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā CostQuery is per-repo (region resolved from the repo's account),        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā dispatched like StatisticsQuery.                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - pricing.json currently has no storagePerGBPerMonth for the archive    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tier ‚ÄĒ must be added (design handoff: ~0.0010), since the cost-by-tier  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā view needs all four tiers.                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Cost is a separate CostQuery (not folded into the fingerprint-cached  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā StatisticsDto), and all cost math happens in Core ‚ÄĒ the CostQuery       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā handler composes the StatisticsQuery outcome with the region's rates    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā and returns finished numbers. The frontend does no arithmetic. Mediator ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 3.0.2 exposes IQuery<T>/IQueryHandler<,> (used here; the codebase's     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā existing queries happen to use ICommand/IStreamQuery, but IQuery is the ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā read-correct interface and mediator.Send handles it identically).       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Data ownership (who owns the calculation)                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā Group 2 ‚ÄĒ Region-aware Cost Calculator                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 2a. CostQuery Mediator query ‚ÄĒ calculation in Core (uses IQuery)        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - New src/Arius.Core/Features/CostQuery/CostQuery.cs:                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - record CostQuery(string? Region, string? Version = null, bool       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā EnsureFullCoverage = false) : IQuery<RepositoryStorageCost>;            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - record RepositoryStorageCost(string Region, string Currency,        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā IReadOnlyList<TierStorageCost> Tiers, double TotalPerMonth);            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - record TierStorageCost(string Tier, long StoredSize, long           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā UniqueChunks, double CostPerMonth);                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - CostQueryHandler : IQueryHandler<CostQuery, RepositoryStorageCost>  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā injects IMediator + PricingCatalog. It dispatches                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā StatisticsQuery(Version, EnsureFullCoverage) to get StoredByTier,       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā resolves the region via PricingCatalog.GetRegion(Region), and for each  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tier computes CostPerMonth = (StoredSize / 1024¬≥) *                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā region.<tier>.StoragePerGbMonth (same GiB convention as                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā RestoreCostCalculator), summing into TotalPerMonth. Returns finished    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā numbers ‚ÄĒ no client math.                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Register in src/Arius.Core/ServiceCollectionExtensions.cs next to the ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā StatisticsQuery handler (~line¬†177):                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā services.AddSingleton<IQueryHandler<CostQuery,                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā RepositoryStorageCost>>(sp => new                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā CostQueryHandler(sp.GetRequiredService<IMediator>(), <PricingCatalog>,  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā logger)). (The per-repo provider already has IMediator + the            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā StatisticsQuery handler registered, so the in-handler Send resolves.)   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - This is the "another cost calculator, exposed via a Mediator          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā CostQuery." RestoreCostCalculator is kept as the restore-only           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā calculator; both now read the same shared PricingCatalog (which "owns   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā the pricing json").                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā

‚Źļ The plan is now fully consistent with both refinements. Re-presenting for
  approval.

  Summary of the two changes you asked for:
  - Cost now rides on StatisticsQuery (one query, one /stats endpoint, one
  cached payload) instead of a separate query. The StatisticsQuery handler
  computes per-tier sizes as today, then calls a new Core StorageCostCalculator
  to attach costPerMonth per tier + a grand total + currency ‚ÄĒ all math in Core,
  frontend renders only. RestoreCostCalculator stays as-is; both share the
  region-keyed PricingCatalog that owns pricing.json.
  - StatisticsQuery switches ICommand<T> ‚Üí IQuery<T> (and handler ‚Üí
  IQueryHandler<,>). Small, contained blast radius: the type def, the
  ServiceCollectionExtensions.cs:177 registration, and
  StatisticsQueryHandlerTests.cs (which constructs the handler directly).
  - Region freshness is handled by invalidating the stats cache on 
  account-region change (account PATCH ‚Üí evict + ClearStatisticsCache for that
  account's repos), since the cache key is region-independent.

‚Źļ User approved Claude's plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†Plan saved to: ~/.claude/plans/1-in-the-overview-lexical-dijkstra.md ¬∑ 
     /plan to edit
     Plan: Storage Accounts management + region-aware Cost Calculator

     Context

     Two related changes to the Arius.Web Angular SPA and its Arius.Api / 
     Arius.Core .NET backend (Mediator/CQRS, SQLite app DB):

     - Group 1 ‚ÄĒ Storage accounts & repos: Today storage accounts are
     second-class ‚ÄĒ they're only created inline in the New/Add-repo wizards, can
     never be edited, and carry no Azure region. The Overview has no place to
     see or manage them. Meanwhile the repo Properties page shows an "Account
     key" field that doesn't even belong to a repo (and isn't persisted). We
     surface accounts on the Overview, add a region to each account, make
     accounts editable via a flyout, and clean up the Properties page.
     - Group 2 ‚ÄĒ Cost calculator: The Statistics tab's "Stored size by tier"
     section shows size but no cost. We add a region-aware StorageCostCalculator
     in Core (a sibling to ‚ÄĒ not a replacement for ‚ÄĒ the existing
     RestoreCostCalculator), fold its output into the StatisticsQuery result
     (switched to IQuery<T>), and add a shared Angular CostCalculator component
     that renders the redesigned cost-aware tier breakdown (per the design
     handoff in scratchpad/design_handoff/.../Statistics Tab v2.dc.html).

     Decisions confirmed with the user

     1. Region pricing = "only regions in the json." pricing.json becomes
     region-keyed and is the single source of truth. The region dropdown lists
     exactly the regions present in the json + an "Unknown / Not in list"
     option. Today that means [westeurope, Unknown]; the list grows as regions
     are added to the json. Rates select by the account's region;
     Unknown/missing ‚Üí fall back to the default region.
     2. Local-path picker = server-side browser. A new backend endpoint lists
     directories as the Arius.Api host/container sees them (mounted volumes
     under Docker; real folders when run locally). A [...] button opens a small
     folder picker over that.

     Key facts that shape the plan (verified)

     - Account key is already account-scoped in the DB
     (storage_accounts.account_key) and the API DTOs. The repo Properties
     "Account key" field is vestigial ‚ÄĒ save() never sends it. So Group 1 #2's
     "reflect in the DB" needs no DB change; it's a frontend removal.
     - No UpdateAccount exists (DB method, endpoint, or DTO) and no location 
     column ‚ÄĒ both are net-new for the edit-account flyout + region.
     - Mediator lives only per-repo (AddMediator() in
     RepositoryProviderRegistry.BuildAsync). The regions list (used during
     account creation, before any repo) must be a plain app-level endpoint
     reading the embedded pricing.json. Cost is per-repo (region resolved from
     the repo's account at the API layer and passed into StatisticsQuery), which
     is already dispatched through the per-repo provider.
     - pricing.json currently has no storagePerGBPerMonth for the archive tier ‚ÄĒ
     must be added (design handoff: ~0.0010), since the cost-by-tier view needs
     all four tiers.
     - Cost is folded into StatisticsQuery (one query, one /stats endpoint, one
     cached payload) rather than a separate query, and all cost math happens in 
     Core. StatisticsQuery is switched to IQuery<T> (Mediator 3.0.2 exposes
     IQuery/IQueryHandler; the codebase's other queries use
     ICommand/IStreamQuery, but IQuery is the read-correct interface and
     mediator.Send handles it identically). Because the stats payload is
     memoized in the app DB keyed by snapshot fingerprint (region-independent),
     the cache is invalidated when an account's region changes (account PATCH ‚Üí
     evict + ClearStatisticsCache for that account's repos).

     Data ownership (who owns the calculation)

     ‚ĒĆ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēź
     ‚Ēā        Concern        ‚Ēā                      Owner                      ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§

     ---
     Group 1 ‚ÄĒ Storage Accounts, Repos, Properties

     1a. Region-keyed pricing as the single source of truth (backend)

     - Move src/Arius.Core/Features/RestoreCommand/pricing.json ‚Üí
     src/Arius.Core/Shared/Pricing/pricing.json; update the <EmbeddedResource>
     path in src/Arius.Core/Arius.Core.csproj.
     - Restructure to region-keyed, add currency per region, and add the missing
     archive storagePerGBPerMonth:
     { "regions": { "westeurope": {
         "currency": "EUR",
         "archive": { "retrievalPerGB":0.0204, "retrievalHighPerGB":0.1102,
     "readOpsPer10000":6.6094, "readOpsHighPer10000":71.6011,
     "storagePerGBPerMonth":0.0010 },
         "hot":  { "writeOpsPer10000":0.05, "storagePerGBPerMonth":0.018 },
         "cool": { "writeOpsPer10000":0.10, "storagePerGBPerMonth":0.01 },
         "cold": { "writeOpsPer10000":0.18, "storagePerGBPerMonth":0.0045 } } }
     }
     - Refactor PricingConfig (currently internal sealed record in
     RestoreCostCalculator.cs) into
     src/Arius.Core/Shared/Pricing/PricingCatalog.cs:
       - PricingCatalog.LoadEmbedded() ‚Üí
     IReadOnlyDictionary<string,RegionPricing> Regions, IReadOnlyList<string> 
     RegionNames, and RegionPricing GetRegion(string? region) (returns the
     region's rates; falls back to the default ‚ÄĒ first/westeurope ‚ÄĒ when
     null/"Unknown"/missing). Keep the existing LoadEmbedded resource-stream
     idiom.
       - RegionPricing holds Currency + the four tiers (same fields as today,
     plus archive storage rate).
     - RestoreCostCalculator stays as the restore-only calculator but consumes
     the new shape (GetRegion(default) ‚Üí identical numbers for WE). Minimal
     change; behavior preserved.

     1b. Account location end-to-end (backend)

     - src/Arius.Api/AppData/AppDatabase.cs: add location TEXT to the
     storage_accounts CREATE TABLE, plus an additive migration in
     CreateOrUpgradeSchema (check PRAGMA table_info(storage_accounts), ALTER 
     TABLE ... ADD COLUMN location if absent). Update
     ReadAccount/ListAccounts/GetAccount, extend InsertAccount(name, key, 
     location), and add UpdateAccount(id, encryptedKey?, location?) using the
     COALESCE($x, col) "null leaves unchanged" idiom already used by
     UpdateRepository.
     - src/Arius.Api/AppData/Records.cs: add string? Location to AccountRecord.
     - src/Arius.Api/Contracts/Dtos.cs: AccountDto += string? Location;
     CreateAccountRequest += string? Location; new UpdateAccountRequest(string? 
     AccountKey, string? Location).
     - src/Arius.Api/Endpoints/AccountEndpoints.cs: include Location in
     ToDto/POST; add GET /accounts/{id} (flyout load) and PATCH /accounts/{id}
     (key+location; secrets.Protect the key only when supplied). For each repo
     under the account: on key change registry.Evict(repoId) (new key takes

     Group 2 ‚ÄĒ Region-aware Cost Calculator

     2a. Extend StatisticsQuery with cost ‚ÄĒ calculation in Core, switch to 
     IQuery

     - src/Arius.Core/Features/StatisticsQuery/StatisticsQuery.cs:
       - Change StatisticsQuery from ICommand<RepositoryStatistics> ‚Üí
     IQuery<RepositoryStatistics>, and the handler from ICommandHandler<,> ‚Üí
     IQueryHandler<,>. Add a region parameter: StatisticsQuery(string? Version =
     null, bool EnsureFullCoverage = false, string? Region = null).
       - Extend the result: add Currency, Region, TotalStorageCostPerMonth to
     RepositoryStatistics, and change StoredByTier from
     IReadOnlyList<ChunkTierStatistic> to a statistics-specific
     IReadOnlyList<TierStatistic> where TierStatistic(BlobTier Tier, long 
     UniqueChunks, long StoredSize, double CostPerMonth). (Leave the chunk-index
     domain type ChunkTierStatistic untouched ‚ÄĒ don't pollute it with pricing.)
       - In the handler: after computing byTier (as today), call the new
     StorageCostCalculator to map each ChunkTierStatistic ‚Üí TierStatistic with
     CostPerMonth = (StoredSize / 1024¬≥) * region.<tier>.StoragePerGbMonth (same
     GiB convention as RestoreCostCalculator), and sum
     TotalStorageCostPerMonth; set Currency/Region from the resolved region.
     - New src/Arius.Core/Shared/Pricing/StorageCostCalculator.cs ‚ÄĒ
     region-aware, owns PricingCatalog; sibling to RestoreCostCalculator. This
     is "the cost calculator that feeds the component," now invoked inside
     StatisticsQuery. Register it as a singleton in AddArius and inject into
     StatisticsQueryHandler.
     - Update registration in src/Arius.Core/ServiceCollectionExtensions.cs
     (line¬†177): ICommandHandler<StatisticsQuery, RepositoryStatistics> ‚Üí
     IQueryHandler<StatisticsQuery, RepositoryStatistics>, and pass the
     StorageCostCalculator into the handler factory.

     erTests.cs: the handler is constructed directly (new 
     StatisticsQueryHandler(snapshot, index, logger)) ‚ÄĒ add the
     StorageCostCalculator arg and assert the new per-tier CostPerMonth /
     TotalStorageCostPerMonth.

      104 +    /// <summary>Adds <paramref name="column"/> to <paramref n
          +ame="table"/> if it is not already present.</summary>         
      105 +    private static void EnsureColumn(SqliteConnection connecti
          +on, string table, string column, string typeAndConstraints)   
      106 +    {                                                         
      107 +        using var info = connection.CreateCommand();          
      108 +        info.CommandText = $"PRAGMA table_info({table});";    
      109 +        using var reader = info.ExecuteReader();              
      110 +        while (reader.Read())                                 
      111 +        {                                                     
      112 +            if (string.Equals(reader.GetString(1), column, Str
          +ingComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))                             
      113 +                return; // already present                    
      114 +        }                                                     
      115 +        reader.Close();                                       
      116 +                                                              
      117 +        using var alter = connection.CreateCommand();         
      118 +        alter.CommandText = $"ALTER TABLE {table} ADD COLUMN {
          +column} {typeAndConstraints};";                               
      119 +        alter.ExecuteNonQuery();                              
      120 +    }                                                         
      121 +

      123      {
      124          var connection = new SqliteConnection(_connectionStrin
           g);

      26 +                                                               
      27 +const CURRENCY_SYMBOLS: Record<string, string> = { EUR: '‚ā¨', US
         +D: '$', GBP: '¬£' };                                            
      28 +                                                               
      29 +/**                                                            
      30 + * Money ‚Üí display string. Whole units at/above 10 (e.g. ‚ā¨182),
         + two decimals below (e.g. ‚ā¨8.14),                              
      31 + * matching the cost-breakdown design. Falls back to a "CODE " 
         +prefix for unknown currencies.                                 
      32 + */                                                            
      33 +export function formatCurrency(amount: number | null | undefine
         +d, currency: string | null | undefined = 'EUR'): string {      
      34 +  if (amount == null) return '‚ÄĒ';                              
      35 +  const code = currency || 'EUR';                              
      36 +  const symbol = CURRENCY_SYMBOLS[code] ?? `${code} `;         
      37 +  const digits = amount >= 10 ? 0 : 2;                         
      38 +  return symbol + amount.toLocaleString('en-US', { minimumFract
         +ionDigits: digits, maximumFractionDigits: digits });           
      39 +}

‚Źļ Implementation complete. Here's what was built and verified.

  Summary

  Group 1 ‚ÄĒ Storage Accounts, Repos, Properties

  - Region-keyed pricing as single source of truth ‚ÄĒ moved pricing.json to
  src/Arius.Core/Shared/Pricing/ (region-keyed, per-region currency + archive
  storage rate), new PricingCatalog (RegionNames, region resolution with default
  fallback). RestoreCostCalculator refactored onto it (behavior preserved).
  - Account location end-to-end ‚ÄĒ storage_accounts.location column + additive
  EnsureColumn migration; AccountRecord/AccountDto/CreateAccountRequest
  extended; new UpdateAccount/DeleteAccount/ListRepositoryIdsForAccount;
  GET/PATCH/DELETE /accounts/{id} (key rotation evicts providers, region change
  clears stats cache); GET /pricing/regions.
  - Server-side folder picker ‚ÄĒ GET /fs/list (browses the API host/container) +
  a shared FolderPickerComponent ([...] button) wired into both wizards'
  local-path and the properties tab.
  - Overview "Storage Accounts" section listing accounts (name / region / repo
  count); clicking a row opens a new edit-account flyout (account-drawer,
  mirrors the properties drawer) to rotate key + set region, with a guarded
  delete.
  - Wizards ‚ÄĒ region <select> (sourced from /pricing/regions + "Unknown / Not in
  list") in the "Add new account" step of both wizards; mandatory fields marked
  with red *; friendly alias optional in the add wizard (defaults to the
  container name).
  - Properties page ‚ÄĒ removed the vestigial "Account key" field; renamed
  "Encryption passphrase" ‚Üí "Passphrase".

  Group 2 ‚ÄĒ Cost Calculator

  - StatisticsQuery switched to IQuery<T> and extended with a Region param; the
  handler calls the new StorageCostCalculator (region + per-tier size ‚Üí per-tier
  cost + grand total + currency, GiB-consistent with RestoreCostCalculator).
  All math is in Core; the API threads the account's region in and the DTO
  carries the finished numbers.
  - New shared CostCalculatorComponent (hero stacked bar + detail table with
  Est. cost/mo + grand-total footer per the design handoff) replaces the inline
  "Stored size by tier" section. The frontend does no arithmetic.

  Verification

  - Backend: full solution builds (0 errors). Tests green ‚ÄĒ Core 622, Api 9, Cli
  150, Architecture 11 (the last required marking the cross-namespace internal
  pricing records [SharedWithinAssembly]).
  - Frontend: production AOT build succeeds (all templates type-check).
  - e2e: updated statistics/statistics-tiers specs for the redesigned markup
  (the per-row "chunks" word moved to the column header); added data-testids
  (account-row, account-drawer, account-region, tier-cost, total-cost,
  folder-browse, ‚Ä¶) for future specs.

  Note: the Playwright e2e and Arius.Integration/E2E suites need a live full
  stack + real Azure storage, so they weren't run here ‚ÄĒ but they compile as
  part of the solution build.

  One thing worth flagging: stale rows in a pre-existing dev .appstate stats
  cache will show ‚ā¨0 cost until the next archive/region change recomputes them
  (they predate the cost fields); fresh DBs and any region edit are unaffected.

‚Źļ You were right on both counts. Here's what I found and fixed, sourced from the
  Azure Retail Prices API (prices.azure.com, product General Block Blob v2,
  LRS, EUR) and verified against Microsoft docs.

  What was wrong

  - Numbers were off. e.g. westeurope archive storage was 0.00086 ‚Üí real
  0.001548; archive read-ops 6.61/71.60 ‚Üí real 5.16/55.91; hot/cool/cold
  write+storage all slightly wrong.
  - Restore formula was incomplete. It only priced archive rehydration. Reading
  from Cool/Cold incurs a per-GiB data-retrieval charge (your example) plus
  per-tier read operations ‚ÄĒ none of which were stored or computed. So a
  cool/cold restore showed ‚ā¨0.
  - GiB vs GB: I checked ‚ÄĒ Azure bills "GB" as binary GiB (2¬≥‚Āį) for both storage
  and retrieval, so the existing 1024¬≥ divisor was actually correct. Kept it.

‚Źļ User approved Claude's plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†Plan saved to: ~/.claude/plans/1-in-the-overview-lexical-dijkstra.md ¬∑ 
     /plan to edit
     Plan: Move Azure pricing into Arius.AzureBlob behind a cloud-agnostic cost 
     interface

     Context

     Cost/pricing currently lives in Arius.Core (Shared/Pricing/* +
     Features/RestoreCommand/RestoreCostCalculator.cs) with an embedded
     pricing.json. But the rates, tier names, retrieval/rehydration/egress model
     and the data are Azure-specific. Arius.Core is the cloud-agnostic core
     (ports); Azure specifics belong in the Arius.AzureBlob adapter (which
     already implements IBlobService/IBlobContainerService).

     This refactor introduces a canonical IStorageCostEstimator interface in
     Arius.Core (provider-agnostic, scoped to our needs) with the Azure 
     implementation in Arius.AzureBlob, so other providers (S3/B2/GCS) can
     implement the same contract. It also commits the pricing.json generator 
     script so the rates can be regenerated.

     Dependency graph is already clean ports-and-adapters: Arius.Core ‚Üí (no
     Arius refs); Arius.AzureBlob/Arius.Api/Arius.Cli/Arius.Migration/Arius.Expl
     orer/Arius.Tests.Shared ‚Üí reference AzureBlob; Arius.Core.Tests does not
     reference AzureBlob (it references Arius.Tests.Shared).

     Decisions (confirmed with the user)

     1. Slim canonical RestoreCostEstimate ‚ÄĒ counts/bytes + currency +
     TotalStandard/TotalHigh. The Azure-specific per-component breakdown
     (retrieval/ops/storage/download/egress) stays internal to the Azure
     implementation.
     2. Single IStorageCostEstimator interface: Regions + EstimateStorageCost +
     EstimateRestoreCost.

     ---
     1. Canonical model ‚ÄĒ Arius.Core/Shared/Cost/

     New namespace Arius.Core.Shared.Cost, all public:
     - interface IStorageCostEstimator
       - IReadOnlyList<string> Regions { get; }
       - StorageCostEstimate EstimateStorageCost(string? region, 
     IReadOnlyList<ChunkTierStatistic> storedByTier)
       - RestoreCostEstimate EstimateRestoreCost(string? region, 
     RestoreCostRequest request)
     - record StorageCostEstimate(string Region, string Currency, 
     IReadOnlyList<TierStorageCost> Tiers, double TotalPerMonth) ‚ÄĒ (was
     StorageCostBreakdown).
     - record TierStorageCost(BlobTier Tier, long UniqueChunks, long StoredSize,
     double CostPerMonth) ‚ÄĒ moved unchanged.
     - record RestoreCostEstimate (slim): ChunksAvailable, 
     ChunksAlreadyRehydrated, ChunksNeedingRehydration, 
     ChunksPendingRehydration, BytesNeedingRehydration, BytesPendingRehydration,
     DownloadBytes, Currency, TotalStandard, TotalHigh. (Drop the per-component
     fields; TotalStandard/High become plain init properties set by the impl.)
     - record RestoreCostRequest: the inputs the handler already accumulates ‚ÄĒ
     per-tier download (Hot/Cool/Cold DownloadChunks/Bytes), archive
     ChunksNeedingRehydration/BytesNeedingRehydration,
     ChunksPendingRehydration/BytesPendingRehydration, ChunksAvailable,
     ChunksAlreadyRehydrated, DownloadBytes, MonthsStored.
     - Reuses existing Core types ChunkTierStatistic (Shared/ChunkIndex) +
     BlobTier (Shared/Storage) ‚ÄĒ BlobTier is already the canonical tier.

     2. Azure implementation ‚ÄĒ Arius.AzureBlob/Pricing/

     - Move pricing.json here; embed in Arius.AzureBlob.csproj
     <EmbeddedResource>, remove from Arius.Core.csproj.
     - Move PricingCatalog‚ÜíAzurePricingCatalog, plus RegionPricing + TierRates
     (stay internal to AzureBlob; drop the [SharedWithinAssembly] once they're
     in one namespace).
     - Move the math from StorageCostCalculator + RestoreCostCalculator into
     AzureBlob as internal helpers. Keep an internal rich AzureRestoreCost
     record (with the component breakdown) so the math stays unit-testable; the
     estimator maps it ‚Üí slim canonical RestoreCostEstimate.
     - public sealed class AzureBlobCostEstimator : IStorageCostEstimator ‚ÄĒ
     loads the embedded catalog once; implements the three methods (region
     resolution incl. "Unknown"‚Üídefault stays here).
     - InternalsVisibleTo("Arius.AzureBlob.Tests") (check/add in AzureBlob's
     AssemblyMarker.cs).

     3. Wiring

     - Arius.Core/ServiceCollectionExtensions.cs (AddArius): add a parameter
     IStorageCostEstimator costEstimator; services.AddSingleton(costEstimator);;
     the StatisticsQuery (line ~181) and RestoreCommand (line ~134) handler
     factories resolve IStorageCostEstimator from sp. Remove the
     StorageCostCalculator registration (line ~179).
     - StatisticsQueryHandler ctor: StorageCostCalculator ‚Üí
     IStorageCostEstimator; call EstimateStorageCost, map to
     RepositoryStatistics.
     - RestoreCommandHandler ctor: add IStorageCostEstimator; replace the
     internal new RestoreCostCalculator(PricingCatalog.LoadEmbedded()‚Ä¶) with
     costEstimator.EstimateRestoreCost(opts.Region, request); keep the
     TotalStandard > 0 gate. JobRunner + frontend unchanged (slim estimate keeps
     every field they read).
     - Update the 6 AddArius call sites to pass the estimator:
     RepositoryProviderRegistry (Api ‚ÄĒ inject the app singleton via ctor),
     CliBuilder, Arius.Migration/Program.cs,
     Arius.Explorer/Infrastructure/RepositorySession.cs, and the two test call
     sites. Production callers already reference AzureBlob ‚Üí pass new 
     AzureBlobCostEstimator() (or the injected singleton).
     - Arius.Api/Program.cs: register IStorageCostEstimator ‚Üí
     AzureBlobCostEstimator singleton. PricingEndpoints injects it for Regions
     (replaces the static PricingCatalog.LoadEmbedded().RegionNames).

     4. Tests

     - Move RestoreCostCalculatorTests + PricingConfigTests from
     Arius.Core.Tests ‚Üí Arius.AzureBlob.Tests, retargeted to
     AzureBlobCostEstimator + its internal AzureRestoreCost/catalog (real
     pricing.json). Keeps the component-level + egress + per-tier assertions,
     now in the adapter that owns them.
     - Add FakeStorageCostEstimator to Arius.Tests.Shared (deterministic
     IStorageCostEstimator).
     - RepositoryTestFixture (Arius.Tests.Shared): expose IStorageCostEstimator 
     CostEstimator (default = new AzureBlobCostEstimator()) and thread it into
     CreateRestoreHandler().
     - StatisticsQueryHandlerTests (Core.Tests): construct with
     FakeStorageCostEstimator (Azure-free, deterministic) and assert the handler
     maps per-tier sizes‚Üícosts + total + currency/region.
     - RestoreCostModelTests (Integration, refs AzureBlob): assert slim fields
     (TotalStandard > 0, TotalHigh > TotalStandard, counts) instead of
     per-component (component asserts now live in AzureBlob.Tests).
     - RestoreCommandHandlerTests (Core.Tests): unchanged except handlers come
     from the fixture (estimator injected); the captured-estimate test asserts
     the slim fields it already uses (counts/bytes).

     5. Generator script

     Commit the Azure-Retail-Prices generator as
     src/Arius.AzureBlob/Pricing/update-pricing.py (next to pricing.json), with
     a usage docstring. It queries prices.azure.com (EUR, LRS, General Block 
     Blob v2 + Bandwidth), covers all standard public commercial regions
     (Gov/MEC/sovereign excluded), and writes the sibling pricing.json. Run:

  Summary

  Both asks delivered: the generator script is committed, and Azure pricing now
  lives in the Arius.AzureBlob adapter behind a cloud-agnostic Core interface.

  Canonical model ‚ÄĒ Arius.Core/Shared/Cost/
  - IStorageCostEstimator: Regions + EstimateStorageCost(region, byTier) +
  EstimateRestoreCost(region, request).
  - Provider-neutral DTOs: StorageCostEstimate, TierStorageCost,
  RestoreCostRequest, and a slim RestoreCostEstimate (counts + currency +
  Standard/High totals). Inputs use the existing canonical BlobTier +
  ChunkTierStatistic. Another provider (S3/B2/GCS) just implements this one
  interface.

  Azure implementation ‚ÄĒ Arius.AzureBlob/Pricing/
  - AzureBlobCostEstimator : IStorageCostEstimator, owning the embedded
  region-keyed pricing.json (moved out of Core),
  AzurePricingCatalog/RegionPricing/TierRates, and the Azure cost math
  (AzureRestoreCostCalculator + internal AzureRestoreCost breakdown).
  - update-pricing.py (next to pricing.json) ‚ÄĒ regenerates rates from the Azure
  Retail Prices API; idempotent. Run: python3 
  src/Arius.AzureBlob/Pricing/update-pricing.py.

  Wiring: AddArius now takes an IStorageCostEstimator; the Statistics/Restore
  handlers resolve it; Api registers the Azure estimator as a singleton
  (powering RepositoryProviderRegistry + /pricing/regions);
  Cli/Migration/Explorer pass it explicitly. The CLI restore table shows the
  slim Standard/High totals. No frontend change ‚ÄĒ DTO/SignalR shapes are
  unchanged.

  Tests: the pricing/cost calc tests moved to Arius.AzureBlob.Tests (real
  pricing.json + internal breakdown asserts); FakeStorageCostEstimator added to
  Arius.Tests.Shared; the Statistics handler unit test now uses the fake
  (Azure-free); the integration restore-cost test asserts the slim contract.
